    This function takes a string as input and returns a list of all the quotation marks in the string.
    '''
    quotation_marks = []
    for i in string:
        if i == '"':
            quotation_marks.append('"')
        elif i == "'":
            quotation_marks.append('"')
        elif i == ' ':
            quotation_marks.append(' ')

            quotation_marks.append('\n')
        elif i == '\t':
            quotation_marks.append('\t')
        elif i == ',':
            quotation_marks.append(',')
        elif i == '.':
            quotation_marks.append('.')
        elif i == '!':

    This function takes a string as input and returns a list of all the quotation marks in the string.
    '''
    quotation_marks = []
    for i in string:
        if i == '"':
            quotation_marks.append('"')
        elif i == "'":
            quotation_marks.append('"')
        elif i == ' ':
            quotation_marks.append(' ')
        elif i == '\n':
            quotation_marks.append('\n')
        elif i == '\t':
            quotation_marks.append('\t')
        elif i == ',':
            quotation_marks.append(',')
        elif i == '.':
            quotation_marks.append('.')
        elif i == '!':
            quotation_marks.append('!')
        elif i == '?':
            quotation_marks.append('?')
        elif i == ':':
            quotation_marks.append(':')
        elif i == ';':
            quotation_marks.append(';

'''Write a function to extract values between quotation marks " " of the given string.'''
def 
'''
def extract_quotation_marks(string):
    '''
    This function takes a string as input and returns a list of all the quotation marks in the string.
    '''
    quotation_marks = []
    for i in string:
        if i == '"':
            quotation_marks.append('"')
        elif i == "'":
            quotation_marks.append('"')
        elif i == ' ':
            quotation_marks.append(' ')
        elif i == '\n':
            quotation_marks.append('\n')
        elif i == '\t':
            quotation_marks.append('\t')
        elif i == ',':
            quotation_marks.append(',')
        elif i == '.':
            quotation_marks.append('.')
        elif i == '!':
            quotation_marks.append('!')
        elif i == '?':
            quotation_marks.append('?')
        elif i == ':':
            quotation_marks.append(':')
        elif i == ';':
            quotation_marks.append(';')
        elif i == '<':
            quotation_marks.append('<')
        elif i == '>':
            quotation_marks.append('>')
        elif i == '@':
            quotation_marks.append('@')
        elif i == '&':
